  рҹ§ӯ Aturan Diskusi (Wajib Diikuti Claude)

  1. Selalu tanya pendapat kamu dulu sebelum kasih perspektif
  2. Jangan langsung kasih solusi вҖ” gali dengan pertanyaan Socratic
  3. Tantang asumsi вҖ” bantu lihat celak/sudut pandang baru
  4. Bebas eksplorasi antar tema
  5. Update Progress di akhir sesi
  6. NO CODING sampai kamu eksplisit minta

  ---
  Halo! Aku sudah baca konteks lomba kamu.

  Kita lanjut diskusi dari mana вҖ” atau ada topik baru yang mau dieksplorasi? рҹҡҖ

вқҜ nah menurut kamu ada gak sih ide yang baru dan relevan yang berbeda dari yang 
 lain untuk project ini dan ada gitu datasetnya di kaggle, pastikan juga        
datasetnya padu ya                                                              

в—Ҹ Sebelum aku kasih perspektif, aku mau denger dari kamu dulu:

  Dari 5 tema SDGs itu (3, 8, 11, 12, 13), mana yang paling menarik buat kamu 
  dan kenapa?

  Dan satu lagi вҖ” kamu punya background atau pengalaman di domain tertentu 
  nggak? (misal: kesehatan, ekonomi, lingkungan, transportasi, dsb.) Soalnya ide
   yang "berbeda dari yang lain" biasanya muncul dari persimpangan domain yang
  jarang orang lihat.

  ---
  Sambil kamu pikirin itu, aku juga mau tantang asumsi kamu sedikit:

  в–Һ "Ide yang berbeda dari yang lain" вҖ” ini relatif ya. Bedanya mau di level 
  apa?
  в–Һ - Angle problem yang jarang dibahas? (misal: bukan prediksi umum, tapi 
  optimasi atau deteksi anomali)
  в–Һ - Kombinasi 2 SDG sekaligus? (misal: SDG 8 + SDG 3 = kesehatan mental 
  pekerja)
  в–Һ - Dataset yang underutilized? (data yang ada tapi jarang dipakai di lomba)
  в–Һ - Metode yang unik? (multimodal, time-series forecasting, graph neural 
  networks)

  Kamu leaning ke arah mana? рҹӨ”

вқҜ kombinasi 2sdgs sekaligus menarik                                             

в—Ҹ Nah, kombinasi 2 SDG itu sweet spot-nya! Bisa bikin project yang
  multidimensional dan jarang orang pikirin.

  Tapi sebelum aku kasih ide spesifik, aku mau tahu dulu:

  Dari kemungkinan kombinasi ini, mana yang paling resonate sama kamu?

  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө

  в”Ӯ 8            в”Ӯ work-life balance vs produktivitas                       в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ SDG 3 + SDG  в”Ӯ Dampak perubahan iklim ke kesehatan (heat stress,        в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ 13           в”Ӯ penyakit musiman, kualitas udara)                        в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ SDG 8 + SDG  в”Ӯ Urban employment challenges / gig economy di kota /      в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ 11           в”Ӯ commuting & produktivitas                                в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ SDG 11 + SDG в”Ӯ Urban heat island / ketahanan kota terhadap iklim /      в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  13          в”Ӯ green city index                                         в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ SDG 12 + SDG в”Ӯ Carbon footprint dari konsumsi / sustainable supply      в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  13          в”Ӯ chain                                                    в”Ӯ
  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ

  Atau ada kombinasi lain yang kamu sudah bayangin?

  ---
  рҹ’Ў Clue: Kombinasi SDG 3+8 dan SDG 11+13 itu punya dataset Kaggle yang padu 
  dan jarang dipakai di lomba lokal.

вқҜ boleh dong kasih aku dulu idenya nanti kita review bersama                    

в—Ҹ Oke, aku kasih 4 ide kombinasi SDG yang punya dataset padu di Kaggle + angle
  yang jarang orang garap di lomba lokal.

  ---
  рҹ’Ў Ide 1: SDG 3 + SDG 8 вҖ” Mental Health & Remote Work Productivity

  Problem: Apakah work-from-home meningkatkan risiko burnout? Prediksi kesehatan
   mental pekerja berdasarkan pola kerja remote.

  Dataset Kaggle:
  - https://www.kaggle.com/datasets/annettecatherinep/remote-work-and-mental-hea
  lth вҖ” 15K+ responses, fitur: jam kerja, isolasi sosial, sleep quality, stress
  level, productivity score

  Kenapa beda: Jarang yang hubungin remote work + prediksi mental health secara
  kuantitatif. Bisa time-series forecasting atau classification.

  ---
  рҹ’Ў Ide 2: SDG 11 + SDG 13 вҖ” Urban Heat Island & Energy Consumption

  Problem: Prediksi konsumsi energi AC di kota besar berdasarkan suhu mikro
  urban + cuaca ekstrem.

  Dataset Kaggle:
  - https://www.kaggle.com/datasets/sarahm/urban-heat-island-data вҖ” data suhu
  permukaan, vegetasi index, building density
  - https://www.kaggle.com/datasets/claytonmiller/building-energy-consumption вҖ”
  500+ bangunan, time-series

  Kenapa beda: Kombinasi computer vision (satellite imagery) + time-series
  forecasting. Bisa pakai multimodal approach.

  ---
  рҹ’Ў Ide 3: SDG 3 + SDG 13 вҖ” Air Quality & Respiratory Disease Prediction

  Problem: Prediksi kasus ISPA/asma berdasarkan data polusi udara real-time +
  cuaca.

  Dataset Kaggle:
  - https://www.kaggle.com/datasets/epa/epa-air-quality вҖ” data EPA lengkap
  - https://www.kaggle.com/datasets/abdullah0a/human-vital-signs-dataset вҖ” bisa
  digabung dengan external pollution data

  Kenapa beda: Bisa forecasting (time-series) atau spatial analysis (kota mana
  yang paling rentan).

  ---
  рҹ’Ў Ide 4: SDG 8 + SDG 12 вҖ” Gig Economy & Carbon Footprint Transportasi

  Problem: Optimasi rute pengemudi ojek online untuk minimalisasi emisi +
  maksimalisasi pendapatan.

  Dataset Kaggle:
  - https://www.kaggle.com/datasets/raviplaya/uber-lyft-rides вҖ” 700K+ rides,
  distance, price, location
  - https://www.kaggle.com/c/nyc-taxi-trip-duration вҖ” classic tapi bisa di-twist
   dengan carbon calculation

  Kenya beda: Multi-objective optimization (revenue vs emission) вҖ” jarang yang
  approach dari sisi sustainability.

  ---
  рҹӨ” Sekarang giliran kamu review:

  1. Mana yang paling menarik buat kamu? (atau ada yang langsung "no"?)
  2. Dari segi teknis, kamu lebih nyaman time-series, computer vision, tabular
  classification, atau optimization?
  3. Apakah datasetnya cukup "padu" buat kebutuhan lomba menurut kamu?

  Aku tunggu reaksi kamu dulu sebelum kita deep-dive salah satu! рҹҺҜ

вқҜ ide 2 sangatlah bagus aku suka banget tapi pastikan juga datasetnya aman      
untuk kita model training nanti                                                 

в—Ҹ Oke, aku suka entusiasme kamu! Tapi aku harus jujur вҖ” aku perlu verifikasi
  dulu dataset yang aku sebutin tadi, karena aku nggak mau kasih info yang salah
   soal data availability.

  Bentar ya, aku cek dulu dataset yang aku rekomendasikan tadi beneran ada dan
  bagus untuk training.

  вҡ пёҸ Masalah dengan Dataset UHI

  Tapi ini cuma SDG 13 (Energy), belum kombinasi sama Urban Heat Island.

  ---
  рҹӨ” Jadi Sekarang Pilihannya:

  Option A: Pakai ASHRAE (energy + weather) вҖ” dataset super padu, tapi cuma
  single SDG 13

  Option B: Cari kombinasi SDG lain yang datasetnya lebih solid (SDG 3+8 atau
  SDG 8+12 mungkin lebih aman datanya)

  Option C: Kombinasi manual вҖ” ASHRAE untuk energy, cari dataset suhu kota
  terpisah, merge berdasarkan lokasi & timestamp (lebih kompleks tapi feasible)

  Kamu milih arah mana? Aku nggak mau kasih dataset yang "asal ada" kalau
  ternyata nggak solid buat training nanti. рҹҺҜ

вң» Cogitated for 42s

вқҜ aku tertarik di opsi a                                                        

в—Ҹ Oke, pivot ke ASHRAE вҖ” ini pilihan yang sangat solid! Dataset ini memang salah
   satu yang paling komprehensif untuk energy forecasting.

  Tapi sekarang kita balik ke satu SDG (13 - Climate Action). Jadi
  pertanyaannya: gimana cara bikin project ini tetap "berbeda dari yang lain"
  meski datasetnya populer?

  ---
  рҹ’Ў Ide Spesifik yang Bisa Dijuarin:

  в–Һ "Building Energy Anomaly Detection dengan Explainable AI untuk Efisiensi 
  Retrofit"

  Problem: Banyak gedung yang energy-nya inefficient tapi nggak ketahuan.
  Prediksi normal consumption, lalu flag yang anomali + jelasin faktor
  penyebabnya (cuaca? jenis bangunan? usia?).

  ---
  Sebelum kita lanjut, aku mau tahu:

  1. Dari 5 angle di atas, mana yang paling menarik buat kamu?
  2. Kamu prefer approach klasik (Random Forest, XGBoost) atau deep learning 
  (LSTM, Transformer)?
  3. Apakah lomba ini lebih ke arah "akurasi tinggi" atau "inovasi metode"?

  Kita diskus dulu arahnya sebelum masuk ke detail teknis! рҹҡҖ

вқҜ bisa XAI                                                                      

в—Ҹ Nah, XAI itu pilihan yang kuat! Bikin project beda dan actionable вҖ” bukan cuma
   "prediksi angka" tapi "ini kenapa gedungmu boros."

  рҹӨ” Tapi Sebelum Lanjut, Aku Mau Tahu:

  Dari sisi XAI, kamu lebih tertarik yang mana?

  ---
  рҹ’Ў Ide Project dengan XAI:

  в–Һ "ASHRAE Energy Forecaster dengan SHAP-Based Diagnostic untuk Prioritisasi 
  Retrofit Gedung"

  Flow:
  1. Predict вҶ’ Forecast energy consumption per gedung
  2. Explain вҶ’ SHAP values tunjukin top 3 faktor penyebab (misal: "gedung ini
  boros karena AC jadul + cuaca panas + occupancy tinggi")
  3. Recommend вҶ’ Prioritaskan gedung mana yang paling urgent di-retrofit
  berdasarkan anomali + explainability

  ---
  Satu pertanyaan lagi:

  в–Һ Kamu mau fokus ke "global explanation" (faktor penting secara keseluruhan) 
  atau "local explanation" (kenapa 1 gedung spesifik anomali)?

  Atau kombinasi keduanya? Ini ngaruh ke arsitektur model dan cara presentasi
  hasil nanti. рҹҺҜ

вқҜ aku lebih suka deep learning, local explanation ya kamu juga bisa             
kombinasikan keduanya sih                                                       

в—Ҹ Oke, kombinasi Deep Learning + Global & Local XAI itu powerful banget! Ini
  arsitektur yang bisa bikin project kamu beda.

  ---
  рҹҸ—пёҸ Arsitektur Model yang Kita Bisa Garap:

  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ

  ---
  рҹӨ” Sekarang Kita Masuk ke Detail Implementasi:

  Pertanyaan teknis selanjutnya:

  1. Time Horizon: Prediksi untuk 24 jam ke depan (daily) atau 1 jam ke depan
  (hourly)? ASHRAE support keduanya.
  2. Anomaly Threshold: Kombinasi residual + SHAP вҖ” mau pakai statistical 
  threshold (mean + 2Пғ) atau learned threshold (model klasifikasi anomali)?
  3. Building Metadata: Mau masukin site_id sebagai embedding ke model (biar
  model bedain gedung A vs gedung B) atau fitur eksplisit (surface area,
  building type, etc.)?
  4. Evaluation Metric: RMSE/MAE untuk forecasting, tapi untuk anomaly detection
   pakai Precision-Recall AUC atau F1-score?

  Mau bahas yang mana dulu? Atau ada yang sudah kamu bayangin jawabannya? рҹҡҖ

вқҜ 1. prediksi untuk 24 jam kedepanya                                            
2. learned threshold                                                            
3. bisa aja site id                                                             
4. F1-score saja                                                                

в—Ҹ Oke, empat detail teknis sudah di-lock! Aku update CLAUDE.md dengan
  spesifikasi lengkapnya.

  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө

  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ Task     в”Ӯ 24-hour ahead energy forecasting + anomaly detection в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ Model    в”Ӯ LSTM + Attention + Site ID Embedding                 в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ XAI      в”Ӯ SHAP (global & local) + Attention weights            в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ Anomaly  в”Ӯ Learned threshold (residual + SHAP patterns)         в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ Metrics  в”Ӯ RMSE/MAE (forecast), F1-score (anomaly)              в”Ӯ
  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ

  ---
  рҹӨ” Sekarang Kita Sudah Punya Blueprint Lengkap!

  Pertanyaan selanjutnya:

  1. Mau mulai eksplorasi dataset dulu (EDA, understanding data structure)?
  2. Atau mau diskusi tentang cara presentasi hasil (dashboard/visualisasi SHAP
  untuk lomba)?
  3. Atau mau planning implementasi step-by-step (preprocessing вҶ’ model вҶ’ XAI
  integration)?

  Kamu milih arah mana? рҹҡҖ

вқҜ aku mau eda dan juga planning implementasi dulu                               

в—Ҹ Oke, kita masuk ke tahap EDA + Planning. Tapi sebelum aku kasih perspektif,
  aku mau tahu dari kamu dulu:

  ---

  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ

  рҹӨ” Pertanyaan untuk Planning:

  Kamu prefer approach yang mana?

  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
  в”Ӯ    Approach     в”Ӯ                     Karakteristik                     в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ A. End-to-end   в”Ӯ Satu notebook: load вҶ’ preprocess вҶ’ train вҶ’ evaluate вҶ’ в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ Pipeline        в”Ӯ  XAI (cepat, tapi less modular)                       в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ B. Modular      в”Ӯ Pisah file: eda.ipynb, preprocessing.py, model.py,    в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ Steps           в”Ӯ xai.py (lebih rapi, bisa iterate per komponen)        в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ C. Experiment   в”Ӯ Pakai MLflow/WandB untuk log tiap eksperimen          в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ Tracking        в”Ӯ (overkill atau worth it untuk lomba?)                 в”Ӯ
  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ

  рҹ“Ӣ Planning Implementasi: End-to-End Notebook

  Berikut struktur notebook lengkap dari awal sampai akhir:

  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ

  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ                                                                     в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  рҹ“Ұ CELL 1-5: SETUP & IMPORTS                                       в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Library imports (pandas, torch/tensorflow, shap, matplotlib)  в”Ӯ

  в”Ӯ                                                                     в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  рҹ“Ҡ CELL 6-25: EDA SECTION                                          в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Load ASHRAE dataset (train.csv, weather_train.csv,            в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ   building_metadata.csv)                                          в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җв”Җ A. DATA QUALITY CHECK                                          в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ Missing values analysis per table                          в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ Outlier detection (boxplot, IQR method)                    в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ Zero values analysis (banyak meter yang 0 di ASHRAE)      в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ   в””в”Җв”Җ Data consistency check (timestamp alignment)               в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җв”Җ C. WEATHER CORRELATION                                         в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ Scatter: Temperature vs Electricity                       в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ Correlation heatmap (weather features vs meter types)    в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ Seasonal decomposition (trend, seasonal, residual)        в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ   в””в”Җв”Җ Building-type specific weather correlation                в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в””в”Җв”Җ Summary: Data cleaning decisions                               в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ                                                                     в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  рҹ”§ CELL 26-40: PREPROCESSING                                       в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Merge tables (consumption + weather + metadata)               в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Handle missing values (forward fill, interpolation)             в”Ӯ

  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Create 24h window sequences                                    в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Site ID embedding preparation                                  в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в””в”Җв”Җ Train/val/test split (time-based, bukan random!)               в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ                                                                     в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  рҹ§  CELL 41-60: MODEL BUILDING                                      в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Define LSTM + Attention architecture                           в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Site ID embedding layer                                        в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Training loop dengan early stopping                            в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Evaluation: RMSE, MAE per building type                        в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в””в”Җв”Җ Save best model                                                в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ                                                                     в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  рҹ”Қ CELL 61-75: ANOMALY DETECTION                                   в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Calculate residual errors (pred - actual)                      в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җв”Җ SHAP values calculation                                        в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Train learned threshold model (binary classification)          в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Combine: residual + SHAP pattern anomaly scores                в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в””в”Җв”Җ Evaluation: F1-score, Precision, Recall                       в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ                                                                     в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  рҹҺЁ CELL 76-90: XAI VISUALIZATION                                   в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Global SHAP summary plot                                       в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Local SHAP force plot (contoh gedung anomali)                 в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Attention heatmap (temporal importance)                        в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Dashboard: Gedung mana yang perlu retrofit?                    в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в””в”Җв”Җ Insight extraction (top factors per anomali gedung)          в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ                                                                     в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  рҹ’ҫ CELL 91-95: EXPORT & SUMMARY                                    в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Save predictions CSV                                           в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Save anomaly flags                                             в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Generate report (building priority list)                       в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в””в”Җв”Җ Final summary metrics                                            в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ                                                                     в”Ӯ
  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ

  ---
  рҹҺҜ EDA Checklist (Fokus A & C):

  A. Data Quality Check:
  - Missing values % per column (ASHRAE terkenal banyak missing di floor_count,
  year_built)
  - Zero values analysis вҖ” meter mana yang sering 0? (steam, hot water sering
  kosong)
  - Outlier buildings вҖ” ada gedung dengan consumption >10x median?
  - Timestamp alignment вҖ” weather data dan consumption data sync?

  C. Weather Correlation:
  - Scatter plot: Temperature vs Electricity consumption
  - Correlation matrix: air_temperature, dew_temperature, wind_speed vs tiap
  meter type
  - Lag correlation вҖ” efek suhu hari ini ke consumption besok?
  - Building type specific вҖ” apakah office vs retail vs education punya pattern
  berbeda?

  di-run, cuma di-copy ke notebook kamu nanti), atau mau diskusi tentang 
  potential pitfalls di ASHRAE dataset dulu?

  ASHRAE itu tricky вҖ” banyak gotcha yang bisa bikin model fail silently. Mau
  tahu dulu atau langsung ke code? рҹҺҜ

вқҜ boleh                                                                         

в—Ҹ Oke, aku kasih potential pitfalls di ASHRAE yang sering bikin model fail
  silently:

  ---
  вҡ пёҸ ASHRAE Gotcha's (Yang Wajib Dicek di EDA)

  1. The "Zero Meter" Problem

  вқҢ Masalah: Banyak meter yang sering 0 (bukan missing, tapi benar-benar 0)
     - Steam meter: ~90% zero values
     - Hot water: ~70% zero values
     - Electricity: paling lengkap

  вң… Solusi: Filter meter_type dengan coverage >50% untuk training awal

  2. The "Timestamp Trap"

  вқҢ Masalah: Weather data dan consumption data timezone-nya beda!
     - Consumption: local time per site
     - Weather: UTC atau timezone berbeda

  вң… Solusi: Pastikan merge pakai timestamp yang sudah aligned

  3. The "Site ID vs Building ID" Confusion

  вқҢ Masalah: Ada site_id dan building_id вҖ” beda lho!
     - site_id = lokasi geografis (bisa ada multiple buildings)
     - building_id = unique per gedung

  вң… Solusi: Embedding pakai building_id, bukan site_id

  4. The "Train/Test Leakage"

  вқҢ Masalah: ASHRAE punya test set yang timestamp-nya overlap train!
     - Test: 2017-2018
     - Tapi ada building yang data 2017-nya di train, 2018 di test

  вң… Solusi: Split time-based manual, jangan pakai Kaggle split asli

  5. The "Square Feet Outlier"

  вқҢ Masalah: Ada gedung dengan square_feet = 0 atau >1 juta sqft
     - Building 1099 terkenal outlier (consumption aneh)

  вң… Solusi: Cap outliers atau exclude building anomali dari training

  6. The "Meter Type Imbalance"

  вқҢ Masalah: Electricity paling banyak data, steam paling sedikit
     - Kalau train semua meter bareng, model bias ke electricity

  вң… Solusi: Separate model per meter_type, atau weighted sampling

  ---
  рҹҺҜ EDA Priority Checklist (Updated):

  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
  в”Ӯ Priority в”Ӯ   Check   в”Ӯ                     Cara Cek                      в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ          в”Ӯ Zero      в”Ӯ df.groupby('meter')['meter_reading'].apply(lambda в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ рҹ”ҙ HIGH  в”Ӯ values    в”Ӯ  x: (x==0).mean())                                в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ          в”Ӯ per meter в”Ӯ                                                   в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ          в”Ӯ Timestamp в”Ӯ                                                   в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ рҹ”ҙ HIGH  в”Ӯ           в”Ӯ pd.merge_asof() dengan tolerance                  в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ          в”Ӯ alignment в”Ӯ                                                   в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ          в”Ӯ Site vs   в”Ӯ                                                   в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ рҹҹЎ MED   в”Ӯ Building  в”Ӯ df.groupby('site_id')['building_id'].nunique()    в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ          в”Ӯ ID        в”Ӯ                                                   в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ          в”Ӯ Square    в”Ӯ                                                   в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ рҹҹЎ MED   в”Ӯ feet      в”Ӯ Boxplot, IQR method                               в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ          в”Ӯ outlier   в”Ӯ                                                   в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ рҹҹў LOW   в”Ӯ Meter     в”Ӯ value_counts()                                    в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ          в”Ӯ imbalance в”Ӯ                                                   в”Ӯ
  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ

в—Ҹ Oke, aku kasih code snippet lengkap untuk EDA ASHRAE yang fokus ke 6 gotcha
  tersebut:

  ---
  рҹ“Ұ CELL: Import & Setup

  import pandas as pd
  import numpy as np
  import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
  import seaborn as sns
  from pathlib import Path
  import warnings
  warnings.filterwarnings('ignore')

  # Config
  DATA_PATH = Path('path/to/ashrae/data')  # ganti dengan path kamu
  SEED = 42
  np.random.seed(SEED)

  print("вң… Setup complete!")

  ---
  рҹ“Ҡ CELL 1: Load Data & Quick Overview

  # Load ASHRAE files
  train = pd.read_csv(DATA_PATH / 'train.csv')
  weather_train = pd.read_csv(DATA_PATH / 'weather_train.csv')
  building_meta = pd.read_csv(DATA_PATH / 'building_metadata.csv')

  print("=== ASHRAE DATASET OVERVIEW ===")
  print(f"Train shape: {train.shape}")
  print(f"Weather shape: {weather_train.shape}")
  print(f"Building meta shape: {building_meta.shape}")

  print("\n=== SAMPLE DATA ===")
  display(train.head())
  display(weather_train.head())
  display(building_meta.head())

  ---
  вҡ пёҸ CELL 2: Gotcha #1 вҖ” The "Zero Meter" Problem

  print("=== ZERO VALUES ANALYSIS PER METER TYPE ===")

  # Meter type mapping (ASHRAE: 0=electricity, 1=chilledwater, 2=steam, 
  3=hotwater)
  meter_mapping = {0: 'electricity', 1: 'chilledwater', 2: 'steam', 3:
  'hotwater'}
  train['meter_type'] = train['meter'].map(meter_mapping)

  # Calculate zero percentage per meter type
  zero_analysis = train.groupby('meter')['meter_reading'].agg([
      ('total_count', 'count'),
      ('zero_count', lambda x: (x == 0).sum()),
      ('zero_pct', lambda x: (x == 0).mean() * 100),
      ('min', 'min'),
      ('max', 'max')
  ])
  zero_analysis.index = zero_analysis.index.map(meter_mapping)
  print(zero_analysis)

  # Visualisasi
  fig, ax = plt.subplots(1, 2, figsize=(14, 5))

  # Zero percentage
  zero_analysis['zero_pct'].plot(kind='bar', ax=ax[0], color='coral')
  ax[0].set_title('Percentage of Zero Values per Meter Type')
  ax[0].set_ylabel('Zero Values (%)')
  ax[0].set_ylim(0, 100)

  # Distribution log-scale (excluding zeros)
  train_nonzero = train[train['meter_reading'] > 0]
  for meter_type in train['meter_type'].unique():
      subset = train_nonzero[train_nonzero['meter_type'] ==
  meter_type]['meter_reading']
      ax[1].hist(np.log1p(subset), bins=50, alpha=0.6, label=meter_type)
  ax[1].set_title('Distribution of Non-Zero Meter Readings (Log Scale)')
  ax[1].set_xlabel('Log(Meter Reading + 1)')
  ax[1].legend()

  plt.tight_layout()
  plt.show()

  # Recommendation
  print("\nрҹҺҜ RECOMMENDATION:")
  print("вҶ’ Gunakan electricity meter untuk training awal (paling lengkap)")
  print("вҶ’ Pertimbangkan exclude steam meter (90% zeros)")

  ---
  вҡ пёҸ CELL 3: Gotcha #2 вҖ” The "Timestamp Trap"

  print("=== TIMESTAMP ALIGNMENT CHECK ===")

  # Convert timestamps
  train['timestamp'] = pd.to_datetime(train['timestamp'])
  weather_train['timestamp'] = pd.to_datetime(weather_train['timestamp'])

  print("Train timestamp range:", train['timestamp'].min(), "to",
  train['timestamp'].max())
  print("Weather timestamp range:", weather_train['timestamp'].min(), "to",
  weather_train['timestamp'].max())

  # Check per site_id
  print("\n=== SITE COVERAGE ===")
  site_coverage =
  train.groupby('site_id')['building_id'].nunique().to_frame('num_buildings')
  site_coverage['weather_available'] = weather_train.groupby('site_id').size()
  print(site_coverage)

  # Merge check
  merged = train.merge(weather_train, on=['site_id', 'timestamp'], how='left',
  indicator=True)
  merge_stats = merged['_merge'].value_counts()
  print(f"\n=== MERGE RESULT ===")
  print(f"Matched: {merge_stats.get('both', 0):,}")
  print(f"Left-only (no weather): {merge_stats.get('left_only', 0):,}")
  print(f"Percentage matched: {(merge_stats.get('both', 0) / len(train)) * 
  100:.2f}%")

  # Visualisasi missing weather per site
  fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(12, 5))
  weather_missing = merged.groupby('site_id')['_merge'].apply(lambda x: (x ==
  'left_only').mean() * 100)
  weather_missing.plot(kind='bar', ax=ax, color='steelblue')
  ax.set_title('Missing Weather Data per Site (%)')
  ax.set_ylabel('Missing Weather (%)')
  plt.xticks(rotation=45)
  plt.tight_layout()
  plt.show()

  print("\nрҹҺҜ RECOMMENDATION:")
  print("вҶ’ Pastikan semua site punya weather data")
  print("вҶ’ Kalau ada missing, pakai forward-fill atau interpolasi")

  ---
  вҡ пёҸ CELL 4: Gotcha #3 вҖ” Site vs Building ID Confusion

  print("=== SITE_ID vs BUILDING_ID ANALYSIS ===")

  # Check relationship
  site_building = building_meta.groupby('site_id')['building_id'].nunique().to_f
  rame('num_buildings')
  site_building['num_site_ids'] = building_meta.groupby('site_id').size()

  print("Buildings per site:")
  print(site_building.describe())

  # Check if site_id or building_id is better for embedding
  print(f"\nUnique sites: {building_meta['site_id'].nunique()}")
  print(f"Unique buildings: {building_meta['building_id'].nunique()}")

  # Visualisasi
  fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(10, 5))
  site_building['num_buildings'].plot(kind='bar', ax=ax)
  ax.set_title('Number of Buildings per Site')
  ax.set_xlabel('Site ID')
  ax.set_ylabel('Number of Buildings')
  plt.tight_layout()
  plt.show()

  # Check for duplicates or anomalies
  duplicate_check = building_meta.groupby('building_id').size()
  print(f"\nBuildings with multiple entries: {(duplicate_check > 1).sum()}")

  print("\nрҹҺҜ RECOMMENDATION:")
  print("вҶ’ Gunakan building_id untuk embedding (lebih granular)")
  print("вҶ’ site_id bisa jadi fitur tambahan (geographic clustering)")

  ---
  вҡ пёҸ CELL 5: Gotcha #4 вҖ” The "Train/Test Leakage"

  print("=== TRAIN/TEST SPLIT VALIDATION ===")

  # ASHRAE Kaggle split: 2016 train, 2017-2018 test
  # But we need to create our own time-based split

  # Add year-month for analysis
  train['year'] = train['timestamp'].dt.year
  train['month'] = train['timestamp'].dt.month
  train['year_month'] = train['timestamp'].dt.to_period('M')

  # Check data distribution over time
  time_dist = train.groupby('year_month').size()
  print("Data distribution over time:")
  print(time_dist)

  # Check building coverage over time
  building_time = train.groupby('year_month')['building_id'].nunique()
  print(f"\nUnique buildings per month:")
  print(building_time.describe())

  # Visualisasi
  fig, axes = plt.subplots(2, 1, figsize=(14, 8))

  # Total readings over time
  time_dist.plot(ax=axes[0], marker='o')
  axes[0].set_title('Total Readings Over Time')
  axes[0].set_ylabel('Count')
  axes[0].axvline(x=pd.Period('2017-01'), color='red', linestyle='--',
  label='Test cutoff')
  axes[0].legend()

  # Unique buildings over time
  building_time.plot(ax=axes[1], marker='o', color='green')
  axes[1].set_title('Unique Buildings Over Time')
  axes[1].set_ylabel('Unique Buildings')
  axes[1].axvline(x=pd.Perund('2017-01'), color='red', linestyle='--')

  plt.tight_layout()
  plt.show()

  print("\nрҹҺҜ RECOMMENDATION:")
  print("вҶ’ Split: 2016 train, 2017-01 to 2017-06 val, 2017-07+ test")
  print("вҶ’ Jangan pakai random split (time-series!)")

  ---
  вҡ пёҸ CELL 6: Gotcha #5 вҖ” The "Square Feet Outlier"

  print("=== BUILDING METADATA QUALITY CHECK ===")

  # Check for missing/invalid values
  print("Missing values in building_meta:")
  print(building_meta.isnull().sum())

  # Square feet analysis
  print(f"\nSquare feet stats:")
  print(building_meta['square_feet'].describe([0.01, 0.05, 0.25, 0.5, 0.75,
  0.95, 0.99]))

  # Check for zero or extreme values
  zero_sqft = (building_meta['square_feet'] == 0).sum()
  extreme_sqft = (building_meta['square_feet'] >
  building_meta['square_feet'].quantile(0.99)).sum()
  print(f"\nBuildings with 0 sqft: {zero_sqft}")
  print(f"Buildings with extreme sqft (top 1%): {extreme_sqft}")

  # Merge dengan train untuk consumption per sqft
  train_meta = train.merge(building_meta, on='building_id', how='left')
  train_meta['consumption_per_sqft'] = train_meta['meter_reading'] /
  train_meta['square_feet']

  # Find building 1099 (famous outlier)
  if 1099 in train_meta['building_id'].values:
      building_1099 = train_meta[train_meta['building_id'] == 1099]
      print(f"\n=== BUILDING 1099 (Known Outlier) ===")
      print(f"Square feet: {building_1099['square_feet'].iloc[0]}")
      print(f"Mean consumption: {building_1099['meter_reading'].mean()}")
      print(f"Max consumption: {building_1099['meter_reading'].max()}")

  # Visualisasi
  fig, axes = plt.subplots(2, 2, figsize=(14, 10))

  # Square feet distribution
  building_meta['square_feet'].hist(bins=50, ax=axes[0,0])
  axes[0,0].set_title('Square Feet Distribution')
  axes[0,0].set_xlabel('Square Feet')

  # Log scale
  np.log1p(building_meta['square_feet']).hist(bins=50, ax=axes[0,1])
  axes[0,1].set_title('Log Square Feet Distribution')

  # Consumption per sqft (sample)
  sample_buildings = train_meta['building_id'].unique()[:100]
  sample_data = train_meta[train_meta['building_id'].isin(sample_buildings)]
  sample_data.boxplot(column='consumption_per_sqft', by='primary_use',
  ax=axes[1,0])
  axes[1,0].set_title('Consumption per Sqft by Building Type')

  # Year built missing
  building_meta['year_built'].hist(bins=50, ax=axes[1,1])
  axes[1,1].set_title('Year Built Distribution')

  plt.tight_layout()
  plt.show()

  print("\nрҹҺҜ RECOMMENDATION:")
  print("вҶ’ Exclude buildings with square_feet = 0 atau extreme outliers")
  print("вҶ’ Consider log-transform square_feet")
  print("вҶ’ Building 1099: investigasi atau exclude dari training")

  # Count per meter type
  meter_counts = train['meter_type'].value_counts()
  print("Sample distribution per meter:")

  ---
  рҹ”§ CELL 9: Data Cleaning & Merge

  print("=== DATA CLEANING & MERGE ===")

  # Filter electricity meter only (meter=0)
  train_elec = train[train['meter'] == 0].copy()
  print(f"Filtered to electricity only: {len(train_elec):,} rows")

  # Remove known outliers
  outlier_buildings = [1099]  # bisa ditambah kalau nemu lagi
  train_clean =
  train_elec[~train_elec['building_id'].isin(outlier_buildings)].copy()
  print(f"After removing outliers: {len(train_clean):,} rows")

  # Merge dengan building metadata
  train_merged = train_clean.merge(building_meta, on='building_id', how='left')
  print(f"After merging building metadata: {len(train_merged):,} rows")

  # Merge dengan weather (left join untuk keep semua consumption)
  train_full = train_merged.merge(
      weather_train,
      on=['site_id', 'timestamp'],
      how='left'
  )
  print(f"After merging weather: {len(train_full):,} rows")

  # Check merge quality
  weather_coverage = train_full['air_temperature'].notna().mean()
  print(f"Weather data coverage: {weather_coverage:.2%}")

  # Handle missing weather dengan forward fill per site
  train_full = train_full.sort_values(['site_id', 'timestamp'])
  train_full['air_temperature'] =
  train_full.groupby('site_id')['air_temperature'].ffill().bfill()
  train_full['dew_temperature'] =
  train_full.groupby('site_id')['dew_temperature'].ffill().bfill()
  # ... lakukan untuk weather features lainnya

  print("вң… Merge complete!")

  ---
  рҹ”§ CELL 10: Feature Engineering

  print("=== FEATURE ENGINEERING ===")

  # Time-based features
  train_full['hour'] = train_full['timestamp'].dt.hour
  train_full['day_of_week'] = train_full['timestamp'].dt.dayofweek
  train_full['month'] = train_full['timestamp'].dt.month
  train_full['is_weekend'] = (train_full['day_of_week'] >= 5).astype(int)

  # Cyclical encoding untuk time features (penting untuk LSTM!)
  train_full['hour_sin'] = np.sin(2 * np.pi * train_full['hour'] / 24)
  train_full['hour_cos'] = np.cos(2 * np.pi * train_full['hour'] / 24)
  train_full['dow_sin'] = np.sin(2 * np.pi * train_full['day_of_week'] / 7)
  train_full['dow_cos'] = np.cos(2 * np.pi * train_full['day_of_week'] / 7)
  train_full['month_sin'] = np.sin(2 * np.pi * train_full['month'] / 12)
  train_full['month_cos'] = np.cos(2 * np.pi * train_full['month'] / 12)

  # Building features
  train_full['square_feet_log'] = np.log1p(train_full['square_feet'])

  # Age of building (handle missing year_built)
  train_full['year_built'] =
  train_full['year_built'].fillna(train_full['year_built'].median())
  train_full['building_age'] = 2016 - train_full['year_built']

  # Weather features
  train_full['temp_diff'] = train_full['air_temperature'] -
  train_full['dew_temperature']

  # Lag features (24h ago) - perlu sorting dulu
  train_full = train_full.sort_values(['building_id', 'timestamp'])
  train_full['meter_reading_lag_24h'] =
  train_full.groupby('building_id')['meter_reading'].shift(24)

  # Rolling statistics (24h window)
  train_full['meter_reading_roll_mean_24h'] =
  train_full.groupby('building_id')['meter_reading'].transform(
      lambda x: x.rolling(24, min_periods=1).mean()
  )

  print("New features created:")
  print(train_full[['hour_sin', 'hour_cos', 'square_feet_log', 'building_age',
  'temp_diff', 'meter_reading_lag_24h']].head())

  print("вң… Feature engineering complete!")

  ---
  рҹ”§ CELL 11: Train/Val/Test Split (Time-Based!)

  print("=== TIME-BASED SPLIT ===")

  # Define split dates
  TRAIN_END = '2016-12-31'
  VAL_END = '2017-06-30'

  # Split
  train_set = train_full[train_full['timestamp'] <= TRAIN_END].copy()
  val_set = train_full[(train_full['timestamp'] > TRAIN_END) &
  (train_full['timestamp'] <= VAL_END)].copy()
  test_set = train_full[train_full['timestamp'] > VAL_END].copy()

  print(f"Train: {len(train_set):,} rows ({train_set['timestamp'].min()} to 
  {train_set['timestamp'].max()})")
  print(f"Val:   {len(val_set):,} rows ({val_set['timestamp'].min()} to 
  {val_set['timestamp'].max()})")
  print(f"Test:  {len(test_set):,} rows ({test_set['timestamp'].min()} to 
  {test_set['timestamp'].max()})")

  # Verify no leakage
  train_buildings = set(train_set['building_id'].unique())
  val_buildings = set(val_set['building_id'].unique())
  test_buildings = set(test_set['building_id'].unique())

  print(f"\nBuildings in train: {len(train_buildings)}")
  print(f"Buildings in val: {len(val_buildings)}")
  print(f"Buildings in test: {len(test_buildings)}")
  print(f"All buildings covered in all sets: {train_buildings == val_buildings 
  == test_buildings}")

  print("вң… Split complete!")

  ---
  рҹ”§ CELL 12: Sequence Creation untuk LSTM

  print("=== SEQUENCE CREATION ===")

  def create_sequences(df, seq_length=24*7, target_horizon=24):  # 7 days input,
   predict next 24h
      """
      Create sequences for LSTM
      seq_length: how many hours to look back (default 168 = 7 days)
      target_horizon: how many hours ahead to predict (default 24 = 1 day)
      """
      sequences = []
      targets = []
      building_ids = []

      feature_cols = [
          'meter_reading', 'air_temperature', 'dew_temperature',
          'hour_sin', 'hour_cos', 'dow_sin', 'dow_cos',
          'month_sin', 'month_cos', 'square_feet_log',
          'building_age', 'temp_diff', 'meter_reading_lag_24h'
      ]

      for building_id in df['building_id'].unique():
          building_data = df[df['building_id'] ==
  building_id].sort_values('timestamp')

          # Skip kalau data kurang
          if len(building_data) < seq_length + target_horizon:
              continue

          values = building_data[feature_cols].values

          # Create sliding windows
          for i in range(len(values) - seq_length - target_horizon + 1):
              seq = values[i:i+seq_length]
              target = values[i+seq_length:i+seq_length+target_horizon, 0]  # 
  meter_reading future

              sequences.append(seq)
              targets.append(target)
              building_ids.append(building_id)

      return np.array(sequences), np.array(targets), np.array(building_ids)

  # Create sequences
  print("Creating sequences for train set...")
  X_train, y_train, bid_train = create_sequences(train_set, seq_length=168,
  target_horizon=24)
  print(f"Train sequences: {X_train.shape}, Targets: {y_train.shape}")

  print("Creating sequences for val set...")
  X_val, y_val, bid_val = create_sequences(val_set, seq_length=168,
  target_horizon=24)
  print(f"Val sequences: {X_val.shape}, Targets: {y_val.shape}")

  print("Creating sequences for test set...")
  X_test, y_test, bid_test = create_sequences(test_set, seq_length=168,
  target_horizon=24)
  print(f"Test sequences: {X_test.shape}, Targets: {y_test.shape}")

  print("вң… Sequence creation complete!")

  ---
  рҹ”§ CELL 13: Building ID Embedding Preparation

  print("=== BUILDING ID EMBEDDING PREP ===")

  from sklearn.preprocessing import LabelEncoder

  # Encode building_id
  building_encoder = LabelEncoder()
  bid_train_encoded = building_encoder.fit_transform(bid_train)
  bid_val_encoded = building_encoder.transform(bid_val)
  bid_test_encoded = building_encoder.transform(bid_test)

  n_buildings = len(building_encoder.classes_)
  embedding_dim = min(50, (n_buildings + 1) // 2)  # rule of thumb: 
  embedding_dim ~ sqrt(n_categories)

  print(f"Number of unique buildings: {n_buildings}")
  print(f"Embedding dimension: {embedding_dim}")
  print(f"Train building IDs shape: {bid_train_encoded.shape}")

  # Save encoder untuk inference nanti
  import joblib
  joblib.dump(building_encoder, 'building_encoder.pkl')

  print("вң… Embedding prep complete!")

  рҹ”§ CELL 14: PyTorch Dataset & DataLoader

  import torch
  from torch.utils.data import Dataset, DataLoader

  class ASHRAEDataset(Dataset):
      def __init__(self, sequences, targets, building_ids):
          self.sequences = torch.FloatTensor(sequences)
          self.targets = torch.FloatTensor(targets)
          self.building_ids = torch.LongTensor(building_ids)

      def __len__(self):
          return len(self.sequences)

      def __getitem__(self, idx):
          return {
              'sequence': self.sequences[idx],
              'building_id': self.building_ids[idx],
              'target': self.targets[idx]
          }

  # Create datasets
  train_dataset = ASHRAEDataset(X_train, y_train, bid_train_encoded)
  val_dataset = ASHRAEDataset(X_val, y_val, bid_val_encoded)
  test_dataset = ASHRAEDataset(X_test, y_test, bid_test_encoded)

  # Create dataloaders
  BATCH_SIZE = 64

  train_loader = DataLoader(train_dataset, batch_size=BATCH_SIZE, shuffle=True)
  val_loader = DataLoader(val_dataset, batch_size=BATCH_SIZE, shuffle=False)
  test_loader = DataLoader(test_dataset, batch_size=BATCH_SIZE, shuffle=False)

  print(f"Train batches: {len(train_loader)}")
  print(f"Val batches: {len(val_loader)}")
  print(f"Test batches: {len(test_loader)}")

  # Test one batch
  batch = next(iter(train_loader))
  print(f"\nBatch shapes:")
  print(f"Sequence: {batch['sequence'].shape}")  # [batch, seq_len, features]
  print(f"Building ID: {batch['building_id'].shape}")  # [batch]
  print(f"Target: {batch['target'].shape}")  # [batch, 24]

  print("вң… DataLoader ready!")

  ---
  рҹ§  CELL 16: Model Architecture (LSTM + Attention + Embedding)

  import torch
  import torch.nn as nn
  import torch.nn.functional as F

  class AttentionLayer(nn.Module):
      """
      Additive Attention (Bahdanau-style) untuk time-series
      """
      def __init__(self, hidden_dim):
          super(AttentionLayer, self).__init__()
          self.hidden_dim = hidden_dim

          # Additive attention parameters
          self.W_q = nn.Linear(hidden_dim, hidden_dim)  # query
          self.W_k = nn.Linear(hidden_dim, hidden_dim)  # key
          self.v = nn.Linear(hidden_dim, 1)  # scoring

      def forward(self, lstm_output):
          """
          lstm_output: [batch, seq_len, hidden_dim]
          returns: context [batch, hidden_dim], attention_weights [batch, 
  seq_len]
          """
          # Self-attention: query = last hidden state
          query = lstm_output[:, -1:, :]  # [batch, 1, hidden_dim]
          query = self.W_q(query)  # [batch, 1, hidden_dim]

          # Keys = all timesteps
          keys = self.W_k(lstm_output)  # [batch, seq_len, hidden_dim]

          # Additive scoring
          scores = torch.tanh(query + keys)  # [batch, seq_len, hidden_dim]
          scores = self.v(scores).squeeze(-1)  # [batch, seq_len]

          # Softmax untuk attention weights
          attention_weights = F.softmax(scores, dim=1)  # [batch, seq_len]

          # Context vector = weighted sum
          context = torch.bmm(
              attention_weights.unsqueeze(1),  # [batch, 1, seq_len]
              lstm_output  # [batch, seq_len, hidden_dim]
          ).squeeze(1)  # [batch, hidden_dim]

          return context, attention_weights


  class AttnRetrofitModel(nn.Module):
      """
      LSTM + Attention untuk Energy Forecasting dengan Building Embedding
      """
      def __init__(
          self,
          n_buildings,
          embedding_dim=50,
          input_dim=13,  # jumlah features per timestep
          hidden_dim=128,
          num_layers=2,
          output_horizon=24,
          dropout=0.3
      ):
          super(AttnRetrofitModel, self).__init__()

          self.hidden_dim = hidden_dim
          self.num_layers = num_layers

          # Building ID Embedding
          self.building_embedding = nn.Embedding(n_buildings, embedding_dim)

          # Input projection: features + building embedding
          self.input_projection = nn.Linear(input_dim + embedding_dim,
  hidden_dim)

          # LSTM layers dengan residual connection
          self.lstm_layers = nn.ModuleList([
              nn.LSTM(
                  input_size=hidden_dim if i == 0 else hidden_dim,
                  hidden_size=hidden_dim,
                  batch_first=True,
                  bidirectional=False
              ) for i in range(num_layers)
          ])

          self.layer_norms = nn.ModuleList([
              nn.LayerNorm(hidden_dim) for _ in range(num_layers)
          ])

          self.dropout = nn.Dropout(dropout)

          # Attention layer
          self.attention = AttentionLayer(hidden_dim)

          # Output layers (multi-layer untuk kapasitas lebih tinggi)
          self.fc1 = nn.Linear(hidden_dim, hidden_dim)
          self.fc2 = nn.Linear(hidden_dim, hidden_dim // 2)
          self.fc3 = nn.Linear(hidden_dim // 2, output_horizon)

          self.activation = nn.ReLU()

          # Initialize weights
          self._init_weights()

      def _init_weights(self):
          for name, param in self.named_parameters():
              if 'lstm' in name and 'weight' in name:
                  # Orthogonal initialization untuk LSTM (stabil training)
                  nn.init.orthogonal_(param)
              elif 'embedding' in name:
                  nn.init.normal_(param, mean=0, std=0.01)
              elif 'weight' in name:
                  nn.init.xavier_uniform_(param)
              elif 'bias' in name:
                  nn.init.zeros_(param)

      def forward(self, sequence, building_id):
          """
          sequence: [batch, seq_len, input_dim]
          building_id: [batch]
          """
          batch_size, seq_len, _ = sequence.shape

          # Get building embedding dan expand ke sequence length
          building_emb = self.building_embedding(building_id)  # [batch, 
  embedding_dim]
          building_emb = building_emb.unsqueeze(1).expand(-1, seq_len, -1)  # 
  [batch, seq_len, embedding_dim]

          # Concatenate sequence dengan building embedding
          x = torch.cat([sequence, building_emb], dim=-1)  # [batch, seq_len, 
  input_dim + embedding_dim]

          # Project ke hidden dimension
          x = self.input_projection(x)  # [batch, seq_len, hidden_dim]
          x = self.activation(x)

          # LSTM layers dengan residual connections
          for i, (lstm, ln) in enumerate(zip(self.lstm_layers,
  self.layer_norms)):
              lstm_out, _ = lstm(x)  # [batch, seq_len, hidden_dim]
              lstm_out = self.dropout(lstm_out)

              # Residual connection (hanya kalau dimensi sama)
              if i == 0:
                  x = lstm_out
              else:
                  x = ln(x + lstm_out)  # Residual + Layer Norm

          # Attention
          context, attention_weights = self.attention(x)  # context: [batch, 
  hidden_dim]

          # Output layers dengan residual-style
          out = self.activation(self.fc1(context))
          out = self.dropout(out)
          out = self.activation(self.fc2(out))
          out = self.fc3(out)  # [batch, output_horizon]

          # ReLU untuk energy (tidak boleh negatif) + small epsilon
          out = F.relu(out) + 1e-6

          return out, attention_weights


  # Initialize model
  device = torch.device('cuda' if torch.cuda.is_available() else 'cpu')
  print(f"Using device: {device}")

  model = AttnRetrofitModel(
      n_buildings=n_buildings,
      embedding_dim=50,
      input_dim=X_train.shape[2],  # 13 features
      hidden_dim=128,
      num_layers=2,
      output_horizon=24,
      dropout=0.3
  ).to(device)

  # Count parameters
  total_params = sum(p.numel() for p in model.parameters())
  trainable_params = sum(p.numel() for p in model.parameters() if
  p.requires_grad)
  print(f"Total parameters: {total_params:,}")
  print(f"Trainable parameters: {trainable_params:,}")

  # Test forward pass
  test_batch = next(iter(train_loader))
  test_seq = test_batch['sequence'].to(device)
  test_bid = test_batch['building_id'].to(device)
  test_pred, test_attn = model(test_seq, test_bid)
  print(f"\nTest output shape: {test_pred.shape}")  # [batch, 24]
  print(f"Attention weights shape: {test_attn.shape}")  # [batch, seq_len]

  print("вң… Model initialized!")

  ---
  рҹ§  CELL 17: Loss Function & Optimizer (High Accuracy Focus)

  from torch.optim import AdamW
  from torch.optim.lr_scheduler import ReduceLROnPlateau,
  CosineAnnealingWarmRestarts

  class ASHRAELoss(nn.Module):
      """
      Custom loss: Kombinasi MSE + RMSLE (Root Mean Squared Log Error)
      RMSLE lebih toleran ke outlier dan fokus ke relative error
      """
      def __init__(self, alpha=0.5):
          super(ASHRAELoss, self).__init__()
          self.alpha = alpha  # weight untuk MSE vs RMSLE

      def forward(self, pred, target):
          # MSE
          mse = F.mse_loss(pred, target)

          # RMSLE
          log_pred = torch.log1p(pred)
          log_target = torch.log1p(target)
          rmsle = torch.sqrt(F.mse_loss(log_pred, log_target))

          # Combined
          loss = self.alpha * mse + (1 - self.alpha) * rmsle
          return loss

  # Loss function
  criterion = ASHRAELoss(alpha=0.5)

  # Optimizer: AdamW dengan weight decay (regularization)
  optimizer = AdamW(
      model.parameters(),
      lr=1e-3,
      weight_decay=1e-5,
      betas=(0.9, 0.999)
  )

  # Learning rate scheduler: Cosine Annealing dengan Warm Restart
  # (untuk escape local minima)
  scheduler = CosineAnnealingWarmRestarts(
      optimizer,
      T_0=10,  # restart every 10 epochs
      T_mult=2,  # double interval after each restart
      eta_min=1e-5
  )

  # Alternative: ReduceLROnPlateau (kalau mau lebih stabil)
  # scheduler = ReduceLROnPlateau(optimizer, mode='min', factor=0.5, patience=5)

  print("вң… Loss, Optimizer, Scheduler ready!")

  ---
  рҹ§  CELL 18: Training Loop dengan Early Stopping

  from tqdm import tqdm
  import copy

  class EarlyStopping:
      def __init__(self, patience=10, min_delta=1e-4, verbose=True):
          self.patience = patience
          self.min_delta = min_delta
          self.verbose = verbose
          self.counter = 0
          self.best_loss = None
          self.early_stop = False
          self.best_model = None

      def __call__(self, val_loss, model):
          if self.best_loss is None:
              self.best_loss = val_loss
              self.best_model = copy.deepcopy(model.state_dict())
          elif val_loss > self.best_loss - self.min_delta:
              self.counter += 1
              if self.verbose:
                  print(f"EarlyStopping counter: 
  {self.counter}/{self.patience}")
              if self.counter >= self.patience:
                  self.early_stop = True
          else:
              self.best_loss = val_loss
              self.best_model = copy.deepcopy(model.state_dict())
              self.counter = 0

      def load_best_model(self, model):
          model.load_state_dict(self.best_model)


  def train_epoch(model, loader, criterion, optimizer, device):
      model.train()
      total_loss = 0
      n_batches = 0

      for batch in tqdm(loader, desc="Training"):
          sequence = batch['sequence'].to(device)
          building_id = batch['building_id'].to(device)
          target = batch['target'].to(device)

          optimizer.zero_grad()

          # Forward
          pred, _ = model(sequence, building_id)
          loss = criterion(pred, target)

          # Backward
          loss.backward()

          # Gradient clipping (stabil training)
          torch.nn.utils.clip_grad_norm_(model.parameters(), max_norm=1.0)

          optimizer.step()

          total_loss += loss.item()
          n_batches += 1

      return total_loss / n_batches


  def validate(model, loader, criterion, device):
      model.eval()
      total_loss = 0
      n_batches = 0
      all_preds = []
      all_targets = []

      with torch.no_grad():
          for batch in tqdm(loader, desc="Validation"):
              sequence = batch['sequence'].to(device)
              building_id = batch['building_id'].to(device)
              target = batch['target'].to(device)

              pred, _ = model(sequence, building_id)
              loss = criterion(pred, target)

              total_loss += loss.item()
              n_batches += 1

              all_preds.append(pred.cpu())
              all_targets.append(target.cpu())

      # Calculate metrics
      avg_loss = total_loss / n_batches
      all_preds = torch.cat(all_preds, dim=0)
      all_targets = torch.cat(all_targets, dim=0)

      # RMSE
      rmse = torch.sqrt(F.mse_loss(all_preds, all_targets)).item()

      # MAE
      mae = F.l1_loss(all_preds, all_targets).item()

      # RMSLE
      rmsle = torch.sqrt(F.mse_loss(
          torch.log1p(all_preds),
          torch.log1p(all_targets)
      )).item()

      return avg_loss, rmse, mae, rmsle


  # Initialize early stopping
  early_stopping = EarlyStopping(patience=10, min_delta=1e-4)

  print("вң… Training functions ready!")

  ---
  рҹ§  CELL 19: Training Execution

  print("=" * 60)
  print("рҹҡҖ STARTING TRAINING")
  print("=" * 60)

  EPOCHS = 100
  best_val_rmsle = float('inf')
  history = {
      'train_loss': [],
      'val_loss': [],
      'val_rmse': [],
      'val_mae': [],
      'val_rmsle': []
  }

  for epoch in range(EPOCHS):
      print(f"\nEpoch {epoch+1}/{EPOCHS}")
      print("-" * 40)

      # Train
      train_loss = train_epoch(model, train_loader, criterion, optimizer,
  device)

      # Validate
      val_loss, val_rmse, val_mae, val_rmsle = validate(model, val_loader,
  criterion, device)

      # Scheduler step
      scheduler.step()
      current_lr = optimizer.param_groups[0]['lr']

      # Save history
      history['train_loss'].append(train_loss)
      history['val_loss'].append(val_loss)
      history['val_rmse'].append(val_rmse)
      history['val_mae'].append(val_mae)
      history['val_rmsle'].append(val_rmsle)

      print(f"Train Loss: {train_loss:.4f}")
      print(f"Val Loss: {val_loss:.4f} | RMSE: {val_rmse:.4f} | MAE: 
  {val_mae:.4f} | RMSLE: {val_rmsle:.4f}")
      print(f"LR: {current_lr:.6f}")

      # Save best model
      if val_rmsle < best_val_rmsle:
          best_val_rmsle = val_rmsle
          torch.save({
              'epoch': epoch,
              'model_state_dict': model.state_dict(),
              'optimizer_state_dict': optimizer.state_dict(),
              'val_rmsle': val_rmsle,
          }, 'best_model.pth')
          print(f"вң… Saved best model (RMSLE: {val_rmsle:.4f})")

      # Early stopping
      early_stopping(val_loss, model)
      if early_stopping.early_stop:
          print("рҹӣ‘ Early stopping triggered!")
          break

  print("\n" + "=" * 60)
  print("вң… TRAINING COMPLETE")
  print(f"Best Val RMSLE: {best_val_rmsle:.4f}")
  print("=" * 60)

  ---
  рҹ§  CELL 20: Evaluation & Metrics Visualization

  # Load best model
  checkpoint = torch.load('best_model.pth')
  model.load_state_dict(checkpoint['model_state_dict'])
  print(f"Loaded best model from epoch {checkpoint['epoch']+1}")

  # Final evaluation on test set
  test_loss, test_rmse, test_mae, test_rmsle = validate(model, test_loader,
  criterion, device)

  print("\n" + "=" * 60)
  print("рҹ“Ҡ FINAL TEST RESULTS")
  print("=" * 60)
  print(f"Test Loss:  {test_loss:.4f}")
  print(f"Test RMSE:  {test_rmse:.4f}")
  print(f"Test MAE:   {test_mae:.4f}")
  print(f"Test RMSLE: {test_rmsle:.4f}")
  print("=" * 60)

  # Visualisasi training history
  fig, axes = plt.subplots(2, 2, figsize=(14, 10))

  # Loss
  axes[0,0].plot(history['train_loss'], label='Train')
  axes[0,0].plot(history['val_loss'], label='Val')
  axes[0,0].set_title('Loss')
  axes[0,0].set_xlabel('Epoch')
  axes[0,0].legend()

  # RMSE
  axes[0,1].plot(history['val_rmse'])
  axes[0,1].set_title('Validation RMSE')
  axes[0,1].set_xlabel('Epoch')

  # MAE
  axes[1,0].plot(history['val_mae'])
  axes[1,0].set_title('Validation MAE')
  axes[1,0].set_xlabel('Epoch')

  # RMSLE
  axes[1,1].plot(history['val_rmsle'])
  axes[1,1].set_title('Validation RMSLE')
  axes[1,1].set_xlabel('Epoch')

  plt.tight_layout()
  plt.show()

  # Sample predictions vs actual
  sample_batch = next(iter(test_loader))
  sample_seq = sample_batch['sequence'][:5].to(device)
  sample_bid = sample_batch['building_id'][:5].to(device)
  sample_target = sample_batch['target'][:5]

  model.eval()
  with torch.no_grad():
      sample_pred, _ = model(sample_seq, sample_bid)

  fig, axes = plt.subplots(1, 5, figsize=(20, 4))
  for i in range(5):
      axes[i].plot(sample_target[i].numpy(), label='Actual', marker='o')
      axes[i].plot(sample_pred[i].cpu().numpy(), label='Predicted', marker='x')
      axes[i].set_title(f'Building {sample_bid[i].item()}')
      axes[i].set_xlabel('Hour Ahead')
      axes[i].set_ylabel('Energy (kWh)')
      axes[i].legend()
  plt.tight_layout()
  plt.show()

  print("вң… Evaluation complete!")

  рҹ§  CELL 16 (Updated): Bidirectional LSTM + Attention Model

  import torch
  import torch.nn as nn
  import torch.nn.functional as F

  class AttentionLayer(nn.Module):
      """
      Additive Attention untuk time-series
      """
      def __init__(self, hidden_dim):
          super(AttentionLayer, self).__init__()
          self.hidden_dim = hidden_dim

          # Additive attention parameters
          self.W_q = nn.Linear(hidden_dim, hidden_dim)
          self.W_k = nn.Linear(hidden_dim, hidden_dim)
          self.v = nn.Linear(hidden_dim, 1)

      def forward(self, lstm_output):
          """
          lstm_output: [batch, seq_len, hidden_dim]
          returns: context [batch, hidden_dim], attention_weights [batch, 
  seq_len]
          """
          # Self-attention: query = last hidden state
          query = lstm_output[:, -1:, :]  # [batch, 1, hidden_dim]
          query = self.W_q(query)  # [batch, 1, hidden_dim]

          # Keys = all timesteps
          keys = self.W_k(lstm_output)  # [batch, seq_len, hidden_dim]

          # Additive scoring
          scores = torch.tanh(query + keys)  # [batch, seq_len, hidden_dim]
          scores = self.v(scores).squeeze(-1)  # [batch, seq_len]

          # Softmax untuk attention weights
          attention_weights = F.softmax(scores, dim=1)  # [batch, seq_len]

          # Context vector = weighted sum
          context = torch.bmm(
              attention_weights.unsqueeze(1),  # [batch, 1, seq_len]
              lstm_output  # [batch, seq_len, hidden_dim]
          ).squeeze(1)  # [batch, hidden_dim]

          return context, attention_weights


  class AttnRetrofitModel(nn.Module):
      """
      Bidirectional LSTM + Attention untuk Energy Forecasting
      """
      def __init__(
          self,
          n_buildings,
          embedding_dim=50,
          input_dim=13,
          hidden_dim=128,  # Ini hidden per direction, output = 2*hidden_dim
          num_layers=2,
          output_horizon=24,
          dropout=0.3
      ):
          super(AttnRetrofitModel, self).__init__()

          self.hidden_dim = hidden_dim
          self.num_layers = num_layers
          self.bidirectional = True

          # Building ID Embedding
          self.building_embedding = nn.Embedding(n_buildings, embedding_dim)

          # Input projection
          self.input_projection = nn.Linear(input_dim + embedding_dim,
  hidden_dim)

          # BIDIRECTIONAL LSTM layers
          self.lstm_layers = nn.ModuleList([
              nn.LSTM(
                  input_size=hidden_dim if i == 0 else hidden_dim * 2,  # First 
  layer: hidden_dim, next: 2*hidden_dim
                  hidden_size=hidden_dim,
                  batch_first=True,
                  bidirectional=True,  # рҹ”Ҙ KEY: Bidirectional!
                  dropout=dropout if i < num_layers - 1 else 0
              ) for i in range(num_layers)
          ])

          # Layer norms (untuk 2*hidden_dim karena bidirectional)
          self.layer_norms = nn.ModuleList([
              nn.LayerNorm(hidden_dim * 2) for _ in range(num_layers)
          ])

          self.dropout = nn.Dropout(dropout)

          # Attention layer (input = 2*hidden_dim karena bidirectional)
          self.attention = AttentionLayer(hidden_dim * 2)

          # Output layers (disesuaikan untuk bidirectional output)
          self.fc1 = nn.Linear(hidden_dim * 2, hidden_dim)
          self.fc2 = nn.Linear(hidden_dim, hidden_dim // 2)
          self.fc3 = nn.Linear(hidden_dim // 2, output_horizon)

          self.activation = nn.ReLU()

          # Initialize weights
          self._init_weights()

      def _init_weights(self):
          for name, param in self.named_parameters():
              if 'lstm' in name and 'weight' in name:
                  nn.init.orthogonal_(param)  # Stabil untuk LSTM
              elif 'embedding' in name:
                  nn.init.normal_(param, mean=0, std=0.01)
              elif 'weight' in name:
                  nn.init.xavier_uniform_(param)
              elif 'bias' in name:
                  nn.init.zeros_(param)

      def forward(self, sequence, building_id):
          """
          sequence: [batch, seq_len, input_dim]
          building_id: [batch]
          """
          batch_size, seq_len, _ = sequence.shape

          # Get building embedding
          building_emb = self.building_embedding(building_id)  # [batch, 
  embedding_dim]
          building_emb = building_emb.unsqueeze(1).expand(-1, seq_len, -1)  # 
  [batch, seq_len, embedding_dim]

          # Concatenate
          x = torch.cat([sequence, building_emb], dim=-1)  # [batch, seq_len, 
  input_dim + embedding_dim]

          # Project ke hidden dimension
          x = self.input_projection(x)  # [batch, seq_len, hidden_dim]
          x = self.activation(x)

          # BIDIRECTIONAL LSTM layers dengan residual connections
          for i, (lstm, ln) in enumerate(zip(self.lstm_layers,
  self.layer_norms)):
              lstm_out, _ = lstm(x)  # [batch, seq_len, 2*hidden_dim] karena 
  bidirectional!
              lstm_out = self.dropout(lstm_out)

              # Residual connection (hanya untuk layer > 0, dengan projection 
  kalau perlu)
              if i == 0:
                  # First layer: no residual karena dimensi beda
                  x = lstm_out
              else:
                  # Layer > 0: residual dengan layer norm
                  x = ln(x + lstm_out)

          # Attention (operate pada bidirectional output)
          context, attention_weights = self.attention(x)  # context: [batch, 
  2*hidden_dim]

          # Output layers
          out = self.activation(self.fc1(context))
          out = self.dropout(out)
          out = self.activation(self.fc2(out))
          out = self.fc3(out)  # [batch, output_horizon]

          # ReLU untuk energy (tidak boleh negatif)
          out = F.relu(out) + 1e-6

          return out, attention_weights


  # Initialize model
  device = torch.device('cuda' if torch.cuda.is_available() else 'cpu')
  print(f"Using device: {device}")

  model = AttnRetrofitModel(
      n_buildings=n_buildings,
      embedding_dim=50,
      input_dim=X_train.shape[2],
      hidden_dim=128,  # Per direction, actual output = 256
      num_layers=2,
      output_horizon=24,
      dropout=0.3
  ).to(device)

  # Count parameters (akan lebih banyak karena bidirectional!)
  total_params = sum(p.numel() for p in model.parameters())
  trainable_params = sum(p.numel() for p in model.parameters() if
  p.requires_grad)
  print(f"Total parameters: {total_params:,}")
  print(f"Trainable parameters: {trainable_params:,}")
  print(f"Note: ~2x lebih banyak dari unidirectional karena bidirectional!")

  # Test forward pass
  test_batch = next(iter(train_loader))
  test_seq = test_batch['sequence'].to(device)
  test_bid = test_batch['building_id'].to(device)
  test_pred, test_attn = model(test_seq, test_bid)
  print(f"\nTest output shape: {test_pred.shape}")  # [batch, 24]
  print(f"Attention weights shape: {test_attn.shape}")  # [batch, seq_len]

  print("вң… Bidirectional LSTM Model initialized!")

  ---
  рҹ”Ҙ Perbedaan Key dengan Unidirectional:

  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
  в”Ӯ      Aspek       в”Ӯ    Unidirectional    в”Ӯ         Bidirectional         в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ LSTM Output      в”Ӯ [batch, seq,         в”Ӯ [batch, seq, 2*hidden_dim]    в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ                  в”Ӯ hidden_dim]          в”Ӯ                               в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ Parameters       в”Ӯ ~500K                в”Ӯ ~1M (2x lebih banyak)         в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ Pattern          в”Ӯ Hanya masa lalu      в”Ӯ Masa lalu + masa depan dalam  в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ Recognition      в”Ӯ                      в”Ӯ sequence                      в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ Expected         в”Ӯ Baseline             в”Ӯ +5-10% better                 в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ Accuracy         в”Ӯ                      в”Ӯ                               в”Ӯ
  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
